[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Remote Code Execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in the Apache Commons[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress library through fuzzing testing. The vulnerability is triggered during TAR[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive processing when unrestricted deserialization occurs through Java's [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mObjectInputStream, specifically when processing TAR archive entry names. The fuzzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mCompressTarFuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m identified this as a high-severity security issue with the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassification [0m[32m"com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mCode Execution"[0m[39m.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is classified as a **Remote Code Execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** vulnerability caused [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby **Insecure Deserialization**. The error message explicitly states: [0m[32m"Unrestricted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mclass/object creation based on externally controlled data may allow remote code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mexecution depending on available classes on the classpath."[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Observed Behavior[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the processing of TAR archive entries in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Commons Compress library. The stack trace reveals the following execution [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflow:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer initiates processing through `[0m[1;35mCompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m28[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The execution flows through the TAR file parsing chain:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `TarFile.<init>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructors[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mTarFile.getNextTarEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `TarArchiveEntry.<init>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructors[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeaderUnwrapped[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m1559[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. At the `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, the code triggers Java's native deserialization [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mjava.io.ObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple ObjectInputStream method calls for deserializing data[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The Jazzer security hook intercepts the deserialization attempt at [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mjaz.Zer.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and reports the security finding[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Findings[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Deserialization Point**: The vulnerability occurs in [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m1559[0m[39m, where externally controlled [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata from a TAR archive is being deserialized using Java's ObjectInputStream[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attack Vector**: An attacker can craft a malicious TAR archive file with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecially crafted entry name that contains serialized Java objects[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Security Controls**: The Jazzer fuzzing framework successfully detected this [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability through its deserialization hooks, which are specifically designed to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatch this type of security issue[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Instrumentation Coverage**: The fuzzer successfully instrumented multiple [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclasses in the Apache Commons Compress library, including:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - TarFile and related classes[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - TarArchiveEntry[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - TarUtils[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Various utility classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOUtils, ArchiveUtils, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove the Vulnerable `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` Method[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Delete the entire `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1549[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1564[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This method is the sole source of the vulnerability. It has no [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate use case for TAR archives - entry names should always be plain strings, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnever deserialized Java objects.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove the Call to `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: In the `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeaderUnwrapped[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m1546[0m[39m, remove the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname = [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This call triggers the deserialization. After removal, the `name` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfield will contain the plain string parsed by `[0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which is the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect and safe behavior.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove Unused Imports[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Remove the following import statements that are only used by the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerable code:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m24[0m[39m: `import java.io.ObjectInput;`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m: `import java.io.ObjectInputStream;`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m39[0m[39m: `import java.util.Base64;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: These imports are red flags indicating deserialization code. After [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoving `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, they are no longer needed.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Remove the Vulnerable Test Case[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/test/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveInputStreamTest.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjava`[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Delete the entire `[0m[1;35mtestDeserializeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` test method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m524[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m560[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This test explicitly tests the vulnerable deserialization feature. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter fixing the vulnerability, this test will fail and should be removed as it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests dangerous, non-standard functionality.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is Optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: The fix only removes the malicious deserialization logic [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout affecting any standard TAR processing functionality[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normal TAR entry name parsing via `[0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` continues to work[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All TAR formats [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOSIX, GNU, XSTAR, oldgnu[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain fully supported[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - PAX headers, long names, sparse files, and other TAR features are unaffected[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Security-First Approach**: Complete removal eliminates the vulnerability [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely rather than attempting to [0m[32m"fix"[0m[39m the deserialization with whitelisting [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwhich is notoriously difficult to secure[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Core Logic**: The fix maintains all legitimate TAR archive [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m1465[0m[39m: `name = [0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` continues to parse entry names [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m1489[0m[39m: `userName = [0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` continues to parse user names [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m1520[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1543[0m[39m: Prefix handling for different TAR formats remains intact[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other TAR header fields continue to be parsed normally[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Standard Compliance**: The fix aligns with TAR specification standards where [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry names are simple strings, not serialized objects[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **TAR Reading**: `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveInputStream.getNextTarEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `TarArchiveEntry` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor → `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeaderUnwrapped[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` continues to work, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjust without the dangerous final step[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **TAR Writing**: `[0m[1;35msetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and other setter methods are unaffected[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **All Tests**: Existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcept the vulnerable `[0m[1;35mtestDeserializeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill continue to pass because the fix only removes non-standard functionality[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Evaluation Report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. ✅ Eliminates the RCE vulnerability at the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1559[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. ✅ Removes the insecure deserialization triggered by external TAR data[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. ✅ Prevents ObjectInputStream from being invoked on untrusted data[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. ✅ No longer allows arbitrary class instantiation from TAR archives[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. ✅ Fuzzer will no longer detect the deserialization vulnerability[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m for legitimate users**: Standard TAR archives will continue to work [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentically[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Only affects malicious TAR files**: TAR archives crafted with the [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"eMezilaireseD"[0m[39m userName and Base64-encoded serialized names will no longer trigger[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthis is the desired outcome[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Test removal**: The `[0m[1;35mtestDeserializeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` test will be removed, but this [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests dangerous functionality that should never have existed[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already uses safe string parsing throughout:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m435[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for safe byte-to-string conversion[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mnormalizeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m234[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m269[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for safe string manipulation[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other TAR header field parsing uses safe numeric parsing [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mparseOctalOrBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and string decoding[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix aligns with these existing safe patterns by removing the anomalous [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization code.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Notes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Points:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is a **removal-only fix** - no new code needs to be added[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch must be applied to the initial codebase before any previous patch [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No fuzzing logic, harness code, or test infrastructure should be modified [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcept[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoving the vulnerable test[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix is surgical: only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m changes in [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m files [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m main source file, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m test file[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Verification:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the fix:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer should no longer detect the deserialization vulnerability[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. All existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcept `[0m[1;35mtestDeserializeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should pass[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Entry names will be processed as plain strings without deserialization[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
